<script type="text/javascript">
var userlist = ['gundam_tb','g_tekketsu','GundamSan_Anime','gundam_reco','G_THE_ORIGIN','buildfighters','gundam_unicorn'];
var list1 = 'twitter_list1.json';

j$(function(){
/*
j$.getJSON('http://cdn.api.twitter.com/1/account/rate_limit_status.json?callback=?', null,
function(data, status){
  if(data.remaining_hits == 0){
    //alert('twitterのAPI制限です。時間をおいて改めてアクセスをお願いします。');
    j$(".twetAleat").css("display","block");
  }
});
*/
j$.getJSON(list1,
function(data,status){
  for(var i=0; i < userlist.length; i++){
    var screen_name_check = false;
    for(var j=0;j<data.length;j++){
      if(data[j].screen_name == userlist[i]) {
        screen_name_check = true;
        break;
      }
    }
    if(screen_name_check) {
      var item = data[j];
      if(item && item.status && item.screen_name && item.name && item.id)
      {
        var html = '<div class="tweetUnit">'+
        '                           <div class="twetImg"><a href="http://twitter.com/#!/'+item.screen_name+'" target="_blank"><img src="'+item.profile_image_url+'" alt="'+item.name+'" width="32" height="32" /></a></div>'+
        '                           <div class="twetTxt">'+
        '                           <h3><a href="http://twitter.com/#!/'+item.screen_name+'" target="_blank">'+item.name+'</a></h3>'+
        '                                   <div class="mask">'+
        '                                           <p class="marquee'+i+'">'+item.status.text+'</p>'+
        '                                   </div>'+
        '                           </div>'+
        '                   </div>';
      

        j$('#twitterArea').append(html);
      }
    }
  }

});
});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
var userlist = ['gundam_tb','g_tekketsu','GundamSan_Anime','gundam_reco','G_THE_ORIGIN','buildfighters','gundam_unicorn'];
var list1 = 'twitter_list1.json';

j$(function(){
/*
j$.getJSON('http://cdn.api.twitter.com/1/account/rate_limit_status.json?callback=?', null,
function(data, status){
  if(data.remaining_hits == 0){
    //alert('twitterのAPI制限です。時間をおいて改めてアクセスをお願いします。');
    j$(".twetAleat").css("display","block");
  }
});
*/
j$.getJSON(list1,
function(data,status){
  for(var i=0; i < userlist.length; i++){
    var screen_name_check = false;
    for(var j=0;j<data.length;j++){
      if(data[j].screen_name == userlist[i]) {
        screen_name_check = true;
        break;
      }
    }
    if(screen_name_check) {
      var item = data[j];
      if(item && item.status && item.screen_name && item.name && item.id)
      {
        var html = '<div class="tweetUnit">'+
        '                           <div class="twetImg"><a href="http://twitter.com/#!/'+item.screen_name+'" target="_blank"><img src="'+item.profile_image_url+'" alt="'+item.name+'" width="32" height="32" /></a></div>'+
        '                           <div class="twetTxt">'+
        '                           <h3><a href="http://twitter.com/#!/'+item.screen_name+'" target="_blank">'+item.name+'</a></h3>'+
        '                                   <div class="mask">'+
        '                                           <p class="marquee'+i+'">'+item.status.text+'</p>'+
        '                                   </div>'+
        '                           </div>'+
        '                   </div>';
      

        j$('#twitterArea').append(html);
      }
    }
  }

});
});
</script>
